The practice of swaddling creates a womb-like feeling of safety, which may soothe a crying infant and lead to a more restorative night’s sleep. Swaddling also helps to promote a deeper and longer sleep by reducing the startle reflex that can wake baby so everyone can sleep peaceful and sound all through the night. 100% Cotton Comfort Guarantee: Our Muslin Swaddle Blankets, composed of a single layer of 100% cotton muslin fabric feel gentle on baby’s delicate skin, and are lightweight and breathable for a relaxed comfort. We pre-wash our cotton muslin so you can wrap your little one in a super-soft swaddle blanket from the start. How do I swaddle baby in an Ely’s &Co. Cotton Muslin Swaddle Blanket? Fold down top corner of blanket and place baby in center. Wrap one side over baby and tuck under arm, behind baby’s back. Then, fold up bottom of blanket over baby’s belly. Finally, wrap remaining flap all the way around baby’s body on the back. Easy Care & Convenience: Here at Ely’s & Co., we know new parents need convenient and versatile baby-gear that is also high quality and stylish. Our duo of breathable muslin cotton swaddles featuring pretty prints and calming hues make this set a must-have item for any expecting parent. The convenience of our two-pack gives you the security of knowing you will always have a super-soft, lightweight muslin cotton cloth that can be used to swaddle baby and as a muslin burp cloth, nursing cover, car seat cover, stroller cover, pram cover, changing pad cover, infant receiving blankets, and tummy time blanket. Muslin Swaddle Blankets are easy to care and become increasing softer after each wash. For best results, machine wash item on cold and tumble dry on low heat. Do not bleach.
